 The system of e-way bill will start from April 1
 is nai vyavastha ko lekar logon ke man main kai sawaal uth rahe hai
 Further understand what is the e-way bill and when it will have to be generated and who will need it
 i-ve bill kya he?i-ve bill ek dastavej he
 This needs to be achieved to those people who are supplying goods worth more than Rs 50 thousand through goods and transporters
 vaise to yah ek rajya se duusare rajya main is keemat kii vastu va saamaan ko transport karne ke liye jaruri he, lekin kuch rajyon main antarraji transport ke liye bhi yah anivaary hoga
 However, the system of inter-state transport of goods worth more than 50 thousand rupees will be implemented gradually
 i-ve bill kaise hasil karen?i-ve bill hasil karne ke liye aap ewaybillgst
 gov
 in par pahunch sakate hai
 If you are a registered businessman and you are sending goods worth more than 50 thousand rupees, then you have to fill the Part a EWB-01 form on the site
 vastu supplai karne se pehle aapako i-ve bill praapt karnaa jaruri he
 If the merchant sending the goods is not registered and the business receiving supplier is registered, then he has to fill the Part A's EWB-01 form
 donon hi ke register na hone par, saamaan kii supplai karne vaale transporter ko yah form bharna hoga
 How to get an transporter e-way bill? If a transporter is not registered, he can enroll himself on GST common portal and generate e-way bill for his client
 sarkaar ke mutabik koi bhi shaks, jo apane saamaan va vastu ko transport kar rahaa he, vah bhi jiesti kaaman portal par pahunchakar khud ko enrol kar i-ve bill janaret kar saktaa he
 Necessary condition for e-way bill The first condition for generating e-way bill is that the business is registered on the GST portal
 agar transporter registerd nahin he, to uskaa i-ve bill portal https: / / ewaybillgst
 gov
 in par enrol hona jaruri he
 For this, it is necessary to have a tax invoice, bill or delivery challan and the ID of the transporter transporting the goods and goods
 iske saath hi transporter document number yaa whical number hona jaruri he
 What if there is a mistake in the e-way bill? If there is any kind of mistake in the e-way bill, you will not be able to rectify it
 aisi sthiti main aapako jis i-ve bill main galati hui he, use radd karnaa hoga or nayaa i-ve bill janaret karnaa hoga
 For which items e-way bill is necessary? E-way bill is necessary for all products
 sirf ve utpaada isamen shaamil nahin honge, jo niyam or sarkari adhisuchana kii badaulat isse baahar rakhe gaye hai
 The government has made it clear that in some special circumstances it will be necessary for handicraft goods and goods to be sent for job work even if the value of goods is less than Rs 50,000
 i-ve bill kii validity kitni he?i-ve bill kii validity tay he
 This will depend on the distance to be transported

 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) The best way to improve your retirement after a job is to start thinking today about how you want to live your life after retirement and accordingly make some decisions right now
 ek survey ke mutabik 80 fisadi log ritairement kii planning nahin kar pate hai
 People who do planning also make some common mistakes that have to be suffered during retirement, so let's know about the mistakes that people often make which you should keep in mind during planning
 1
 It is not necessary to know your expenses correctly, it is important to estimate how much your expenses will be after retirement
 yani apni jaruraton kaa sahi anumaan lagaana bahut jaruri he agar aankalan sahi nahin kiya gaya to aapkaa ritairement fund kam pad saktaa he
 So instead of guessing, you should prepare a list of expenses of your last few months and prepare an amount by taking out an average
 2
 Keeping in mind the depreciating value of the rupee, we are all facing inflation, yet we forget it while planning for retirement
 nateeja yah hota he ki mahangaai ke prabhaav ke chalate aane vaale samay main aapkaa fund kam pad jaataa he
 There is a simple fund, the value of rupee today will not last a lifetime, that is, what you are able to buy today for 10 rupees, after 20 years, its value will increase by two to two and a half times
 3
 Continuing to withdraw money from retirement funds Often people think that retirement is far away, in such a time, people withdraw money from this fund whenever needed
 bacchon kii shaadi, admician aadi ke liye to fund se paise nikaalnaa thik bhi he, lekin dikkat to tab hoti he jab log lakjri chizon ke liye jaise car khareednaa, videsh yatra aadi ke liye iskaa istemaal karnaa shuru kar dete hai
 So before joining the retirement fund, be sure to think that this money is for the time when you will not have any means of earning
 4
 Non-maintenance of a separate medical fund: It is necessary to make separate arrangements for medical expenses in the retirement fund as people get more sick in old age
 saath hi aksar kai tarah kii swasth sambandhi dikkaton se jujhate he
 Therefore, one should think about this at the time of retirement planning
 5
 First repay the loan
 One thing that you should always keep in mind is that you should pay maximum debt before retirement
 kyonki ritairement ke baad aapaki kamai kaa jariya khatm ho jaataa he or jindagi keval unheen paison ke dam par chalaani hoti he jo aapane jamaa kiye hai
 Therefore, keep in mind that you do not have to repay the loan from the fund

 angreji akhbaar times of india kii khabar ke mutabik, dilli kii ek sanstha association for democratic riforms ne haal hi ek report jari kii he, jisamen kaha gaya he ki maharashtra vidhansabha chunaav main jin 2,336 ummidavaaron ne kismat aajamaai, unamem se 798 ke khilaaf aapraadhik maamle darj hai
 The report said that out of all the 288 mlas elected, 165 have criminal cases against them
 isse pehle ke aankadon par gaur karen to saal 2009 main 52 fisadi or 2004 main 46 fisadi ke khilaaf aapraadhik maamle darj the
 The current elected 165 mlas have criminal cases against them
 jabaki inamen se 70 fisadi yani 115 par gambhir aapraadhik maamle darj hai, jinamein devendra fadanvis kaa naam bhi shaamil he
 The mlas include serious cases like murder, attempt to murder, kidnapping, forgery and involvement in riots
 bijepi ke 70 vidhayakon ke khilaaf darj hai maamlavidhansabha chunaav main bijepi sabase badi party banakar ubhari he

 " West Indies 'A' beat India 'A' by 55 runs in the second unofficial one-dayer to level the three-match series 1-1, on the basis of all-rounder Jonathan Carter's first century of career and best bowling by fast bowler Miguel Cummins
 She did it
 jonathan carter ne shuru main mili jeevandaan kaa phayda uthaakar 132 gendon par 18 chaukon or teen chhakkon kii madad se 133 ran banaae, jo unke list 'e' kariyar kaa pehla shatak he
 He made 79 for the third wicket with Kirk Edwards (36) and two useful partnerships of 131 runs for the fifth wicket with Leon Johnson (39)
 isse ballebaaji kaa nyotaa paane vaale west indies 'e' ne chah wicket par 279 ran kaa majboot score khadaa kiya
 No batsman played a big innings for the Indian team, who won by 77 runs in the first match and finally the entire team 48
 4 over main 224 ran par dher ho gai
 The 23-year-old Cummins took four wickets for 31, his best performance in List 'A'
 carter ne gendbaaji main bhi kamaal dikhaaya tathaa 33 ran dekar do wicket liye
 Left-arm spinner Nikita Miller contributed to the West Indies 'A' victory with two wickets in his one over
 bharat kii shuruyaat acchhee nahin rahi
 His top five batsmen had returned to the pavilion for 114 runs
 inamen pichley match main shatak jadne vaale yuvaraj singh (40) tathaa ardhshtkeey paariyaan khilne vaale mandeep singh (03) or yusuf pathan (0) bhi shaamil the
 Opener Unmukt Chand (38) did not play a big innings despite spending a lot of time at the crease
 kedaar jadhav (35) or naman ojha (34) teji se ran banane ke dabaav main pavilion laute
 Yuvraj and Unmukt shared a 64-run partnership for the third wicket, but they were unable to score as fast as expected
 unmukt ne carter kii lagaataar gendon par chakka or chaukaa lagaaya, lekin iske baad vah jald hi pavilion laut gaye
 He faced 72 balls before hitting a catch on long on off Ashley Nurse and hit three fours and a six
 baayen haath ke spinner nikita miller kaa pari kaa 28waan over bharat ke liye ghaatak sabit hua
 Yuvraj made a direct catch to Kieran Powell standing on the extra cover in an attempt to drive
 agali gend par pathan asamanjas kii sthiti main slip main kaich de baithe
 Yuvraj, who scored 123 runs in the last match, played 58 balls and hit three fours and a six
 camins ne jadhav or ojha ko out karke bharat kii rahi-sahi ummid bhi khatm kar di
 Earlier in the morning, Indian fast bowler r Vinay Kumar (3 for 56) took full advantage of the conditions
 carabian captain keeran pavel (4) ne unki gend par wicketiper ojha ko aasaan kaich thamaya
 The Karnataka bowler forced Andre Fletcher (15) to take a catch behind the wicket in his next over
 tippaniyan Edwards struggled to score runs after Vinaykumar hit three fours in one over
 unhone 28wein over main pathan kii pehali gend par chakka jamaaya, lekin agali gend aage khilne ke prayaas main chook gaye or ojha ne unhen stump out kar diya
 New batsman Andre Russell (12) hit two sixes as soon as he came, but he caught a catch on long on in this over of Pathan
 west indies 'e' kaa score jab chaar wicket par 112 ran tha, tab carter or johnson ne badi saajhedaari nibhaai
 Both of them waited for loose balls and did not refrain from playing big shots
 vinayakumar ne 46wein over main johnson ko out karke yah saajhedaari todi
 He played 46 balls in his innings and hit three fours and a six
 carter ko aakhir main unadakat ne elbeadblyoo out kiya
 Devon Thomas 13 and Ashley Nurs 12 not out
 teesraa or aakhri match 19 sitambar ko bengaluru main hi khelaa jayega

 unhone kark edwards (36) ke saath tisare wicket ke liye 79 or leone johnson (39) ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 131 ranon kii do upyogi saajhedaariyaan kin
